# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy Stats Scope and Tag Architecture

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the stats system: the Stats::Scope hierarchy, the tag extraction from metric names, the stat name interning (StatNamePool), and the stat sink dispatch for Prometheus and statsd output.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)

\"text\": \"The Envoy Stats system in envoyproxy/envoy v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple tightly integrated components:\\n\\n**Core Symbol Table (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h/.cc)**: The SymbolTable manages a compact namespace for stats using symbol interning. StatName objects represent interned stat names, while StatNamePool provides pooled allocation for groups of related stats. StatNameManagedStorage allows automatic cleanup of StatNames without explicit free() calls.\\n\\n**Stats Scope Hierarchy (envoy/stats/store.h, source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/.cc, source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/.cc)**: The Stats::Scope interface defines the hierarchy for creating statistics. ThreadLocalStoreImpl provides the main implementation with thread-local caching and scope management (ScopeImpl class), while IsolatedStoreImpl provides a simpler, non-thread-safe variant with IsolatedScopeImpl. Both implement the Stats::Scope interface for creating counters, gauges, and histograms.\\n\\n**Allocator & Metrics (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/metric_impl.h/.cc)**: AllocatorImpl creates metric objects (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, TextReadout). MetricImpl and MetricHelper manage the internal representation combining stat names, tag-extracted names, and StatNameTagVectors. Concrete implementations include CounterImpl, GaugeImpl, TextReadoutImpl, and HistogramImpl/ThreadLocalHistogramImpl/ParentHistogramImpl.\\n\\n**Tag Extraction System (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/.cc, source/common/config/well_known_names.h/.cc)**: TagProducerImpl extracts tags from metric names based on regex patterns and fixed values. Multiple TagExtractor implementations handle different extraction strategies: TagExtractorImplBase (regex-based), TagExtractorStdRegexImpl, TagExtractorRe2Impl, TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values), and TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based patterns). Well-known tag definitions are stored in well_known_names.cc.\\n\\n**Statsd Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: The common statsd implementation in statsd.h/.cc provides UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink base classes with tag format support (tag_formats.h/.cc). StatsdSinkFactory, DogStatsdSinkFactory, and GraphiteStatsdSinkFactory configure and create sink instances for different protocol variants.\\n\\n**Prometheus Formatting (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_handler.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_render.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_html_render.h/.cc)**: PrometheusStatsFormatter converts metrics to Prometheus text format with proper tag formatting. StatsHandler and related render classes handle HTTP endpoint responses. PrometheusStatsFormatter::statsAsPrometheus() is the main dispatch point for formatting counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts.\\n\\n**Additional Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: Metrics service sink for gRPC, OpenTelemetry/OTLP sink implementation with OtlpMetricsFlusherImpl, Hystrix sink, and WebAssembly-based sinks. Each sink factory extends the configuration pattern to support different output formats.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**: utility.h/.cc provides helpers for scope/stat creation, histogram_impl.h/.cc implements histogram bucketing, tag_utility.h/.cc handles tag joining with stat names, stats_matcher_impl.h/.cc filters which stats are created, stat_merger.h/.cc merges stats across hot restarts, and deferred_creation.h allows lazy stat initialization.\\n\\n**Public APIs (envoy/stats/)**: Headers define the public interfaces for Scope, Store, StoreRoot, Sink, Histogram, Allocator, TagProducer, and SymbolTable. stats_macros.h provides convenience macros for stat definition. custom_stat_namespaces.h supports custom metrics outside the core Envoy stats.\"\n}\n",

\"text\": \"The Envoy Stats system in envoyproxy/envoy v1.31.2 is implemented across multiple tightly integrated components:\\n\\n**Core Symbol Table (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h/.cc)**: The SymbolTable manages a compact namespace for stats using symbol interning. StatName objects represent interned stat names, while StatNamePool provides pooled allocation for groups of related stats. StatNameManagedStorage allows automatic cleanup of StatNames without explicit free() calls.\\n\\n**Stats Scope Hierarchy (envoy/stats/store.h, source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/.cc, source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/.cc)**: The Stats::Scope interface defines the hierarchy for creating statistics. ThreadLocalStoreImpl provides the main implementation with thread-local caching and scope management (ScopeImpl class), while IsolatedStoreImpl provides a simpler, non-thread-safe variant with IsolatedScopeImpl. Both implement the Stats::Scope interface for creating counters, gauges, and histograms.\\n\\n**Allocator & Metrics (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/metric_impl.h/.cc)**: AllocatorImpl creates metric objects (Counter, Gauge, Histogram, TextReadout). MetricImpl and MetricHelper manage the internal representation combining stat names, tag-extracted names, and StatNameTagVectors. Concrete implementations include CounterImpl, GaugeImpl, TextReadoutImpl, and HistogramImpl/ThreadLocalHistogramImpl/ParentHistogramImpl.\\n\\n**Tag Extraction System (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/.cc, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/.cc, source/common/config/well_known_names.h/.cc)**: TagProducerImpl extracts tags from metric names based on regex patterns and fixed values. Multiple TagExtractor implementations handle different extraction strategies: TagExtractorImplBase (regex-based), TagExtractorStdRegexImpl, TagExtractorRe2Impl, TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values), and TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based patterns). Well-known tag definitions are stored in well_known_names.cc.\\n\\n**Statsd Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: The common statsd implementation in statsd.h/.cc provides UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink base classes with tag format support (tag_formats.h/.cc). StatsdSinkFactory, DogStatsdSinkFactory, and GraphiteStatsdSinkFactory configure and create sink instances for different protocol variants.\\n\\n**Prometheus Formatting (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_handler.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_render.h/.cc, source/server/admin/stats_html_render.h/.cc)**: PrometheusStatsFormatter converts metrics to Prometheus text format with proper tag formatting. StatsHandler and related render classes handle HTTP endpoint responses. PrometheusStatsFormatter::statsAsPrometheus() is the main dispatch point for formatting counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts.\\n\\n**Additional Stat Sinks (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/, source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: Metrics service sink for gRPC, OpenTelemetry/OTLP sink implementation with OtlpMetricsFlusherImpl, Hystrix sink, and WebAssembly-based sinks. Each sink factory extends the configuration pattern to support different output formats.\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure**: utility.h/.cc provides helpers for scope/stat creation, histogram_impl.h/.cc implements histogram bucketing, tag_utility.h/.cc handles tag joining with stat names, stats_matcher_impl.h/.cc filters which stats are created, stat_merger.h/.cc merges stats across hot restarts, and deferred_creation.h allows lazy stat initialization.\\n\\n**Public APIs (envoy/stats/)**: Headers define the public interfaces for Scope, Store, StoreRoot, Sink, Histogram, Allocator, TagProducer, and SymbolTable. stats_macros.h provides convenience macros for stat definition. custom_stat_namespaces.h supports custom metrics outside the core Envoy stats.\"\n}\n",
